    ELSE NULL
END, CASE

    ELSE NULL
END, [t].[Genre], [t].[PosterUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Id], [t0].[FullName], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
FROM (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[DateWatched], [m].[Description], [m].[Genre], [m].[IsWatched], [m].[PosterUrl], [m].[Rating], [m].[StudioID], [m].[Title]
    FROM [Movies] AS [m]
    ORDER BY [m].[Title]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Description], [t].[IsWatched], CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[DateWatched]
    ELSE NULL
END, CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[Rating]
    ELSE NULL
END, [t].[Genre], [t].[PosterUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Id], [t0].[FullName], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
FROM (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[DateWatched], [m].[Description], [m].[Genre], [m].[IsWatched], [m].[PosterUrl], [m].[Rating], [m].[StudioID], [m].[Title]
    FROM [Movies] AS [m]
    ORDER BY [m].[Title]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Studios] AS [s] ON [t].[StudioID] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[FullName], [m0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[MovieId]
    FROM [Movie_Actors] AS [m0]
    INNER JOIN [Actors] AS [a] ON [m0].[ActorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[MovieId]
ORDER BY [t].[Title], [t].[Id], [s].[Id], [t0].[Id]

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Description], [t].[IsWatched], CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[DateWatched]
    ELSE NULL
END, CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[Rating]
    ELSE NULL
END, [t].[Genre], [t].[PosterUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Id], [t0].[FullName], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
FROM (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[DateWatched], [m].[Description], [m].[Genre], [m].[IsWatched], [m].[PosterUrl], [m].[Rating], [m].[StudioID], [m].[Title]
    FROM [Movies] AS [m]
    ORDER BY [m].[Title]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Studios] AS [s] ON [t].[StudioID] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[FullName], [m0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[MovieId]
    FROM [Movie_Actors] AS [m0]
    INNER JOIN [Actors] AS [a] ON [m0].[ActorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[MovieId]
ORDER BY [t].[Title], [t].[Id], [s].[Id], [t0].[Id]

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Description], [t].[IsWatched], CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[DateWatched]
    ELSE NULL
END, CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[Rating]
    ELSE NULL
END, [t].[Genre], [t].[PosterUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Id], [t0].[FullName], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
FROM (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[DateWatched], [m].[Description], [m].[Genre], [m].[IsWatched], [m].[PosterUrl], [m].[Rating], [m].[StudioID], [m].[Title]
    FROM [Movies] AS [m]
    ORDER BY [m].[Title]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Studios] AS [s] ON [t].[StudioID] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[FullName], [m0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[MovieId]
    FROM [Movie_Actors] AS [m0]
    INNER JOIN [Actors] AS [a] ON [m0].[ActorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[MovieId]
ORDER BY [t].[Title], [t].[Id], [s].[Id], [t0].[Id]

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Description], [t].[IsWatched], CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[DateWatched]
    ELSE NULL
END, CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[Rating]
    ELSE NULL
END, [t].[Genre], [t].[PosterUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Id], [t0].[FullName], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
FROM (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[DateWatched], [m].[Description], [m].[Genre], [m].[IsWatched], [m].[PosterUrl], [m].[Rating], [m].[StudioID], [m].[Title]
    FROM [Movies] AS [m]
    ORDER BY [m].[Title]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Studios] AS [s] ON [t].[StudioID] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[FullName], [m0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[MovieId]
    FROM [Movie_Actors] AS [m0]
    INNER JOIN [Actors] AS [a] ON [m0].[ActorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[MovieId]
ORDER BY [t].[Title], [t].[Id], [s].[Id], [t0].[Id]

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Description], [t].[IsWatched], CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[DateWatched]
    ELSE NULL
END, CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[Rating]
    ELSE NULL
END, [t].[Genre], [t].[PosterUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Id], [t0].[FullName], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
FROM (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[DateWatched], [m].[Description], [m].[Genre], [m].[IsWatched], [m].[PosterUrl], [m].[Rating], [m].[StudioID], [m].[Title]
    FROM [Movies] AS [m]
    ORDER BY [m].[Title]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Studios] AS [s] ON [t].[StudioID] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[FullName], [m0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[MovieId]
    FROM [Movie_Actors] AS [m0]
    INNER JOIN [Actors] AS [a] ON [m0].[ActorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[MovieId]
ORDER BY [t].[Title], [t].[Id], [s].[Id], [t0].[Id]

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Description], [t].[IsWatched], CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[DateWatched]
    ELSE NULL
END, CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[Rating]
    ELSE NULL
END, [t].[Genre], [t].[PosterUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Id], [t0].[FullName], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
FROM (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[DateWatched], [m].[Description], [m].[Genre], [m].[IsWatched], [m].[PosterUrl], [m].[Rating], [m].[StudioID], [m].[Title]
    FROM [Movies] AS [m]
    ORDER BY [m].[Title]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Studios] AS [s] ON [t].[StudioID] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[FullName], [m0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[MovieId]
    FROM [Movie_Actors] AS [m0]
    INNER JOIN [Actors] AS [a] ON [m0].[ActorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[MovieId]
ORDER BY [t].[Title], [t].[Id], [s].[Id], [t0].[Id]

    ELSE NULL
END, CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[Rating]
    ELSE NULL
END, [t].[Genre], [t].[PosterUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Id], [t0].[FullName], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
FROM (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[DateWatched], [m].[Description], [m].[Genre], [m].[IsWatched], [m].[PosterUrl], [m].[Rating], [m].[StudioID], [m].[Title]
    FROM [Movies] AS [m]
    ORDER BY [m].[Title]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Studios] AS [s] ON [t].[StudioID] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[FullName], [m0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[MovieId]
    FROM [Movie_Actors] AS [m0]
    INNER JOIN [Actors] AS [a] ON [m0].[ActorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[MovieId]

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Description], [t].[IsWatched], CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[DateWatched]
    ELSE NULL
END, CASE
    WHEN [t].[IsWatched] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [t].[Rating]
    ELSE NULL
END, [t].[Genre], [t].[PosterUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Id], [t0].[FullName], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]
FROM (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[DateWatched], [m].[Description], [m].[Genre], [m].[IsWatched], [m].[PosterUrl], [m].[Rating], [m].[StudioID], [m].[Title]
    FROM [Movies] AS [m]
    ORDER BY [m].[Title]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Studios] AS [s] ON [t].[StudioID] = [s].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[FullName], [m0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[MovieId]
    FROM [Movie_Actors] AS [m0]
    INNER JOIN [Actors] AS [a] ON [m0].[ActorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[MovieId]
